< Text>
Vibe Organic Kitchen serves the most beautiful food I have ever eaten, and ALL of it is organic, gluten free, and vegan. This is mind blowing to me. I‚Äôm not vegan, but I do have to order gluten free, vegan foods because my daughter is allergic to dairy and eggs. Thus, I found Vibe Organic Kitchen and gave it a try! The Cobb Salad, the Macro Bowl, the Taco Fiesta Toast, and the Avocado Toast are incredible! I ordered these items every day. The colorful, beautiful food could turn me into a vegan if I lived here. Truly excellent! Thanks for your spectacular, delicious food, Vibe!</Text>

< text>
We tried the breakfast bowl, macro bowl, and Mediterranean bowl. All were a fantastic flavorful dance on our taste buds. My non vegan family wasn't missing the meat at all. They have sparkling water free on tap which I thought was an amazing touch. Staff was friendly. I don't think you can go wrong with any of their dishes. I saw people eating the tacos and they looked so good im going to try them next time. They also have smoothies, juices, and burgers. Everything is plant based and vegan. Im so grateful this place exists. It's hour away from me but I will definitely be going back!< /text>

The Pit Toilets are boarded up!! Please remember to bring toilet paper and be prepared to pack out your toilet paper. <review>Beautiful campground. It's a 2 or 3 mile hike to get there so it's clean because the trashy messy people are too lazy to hike in that far. Make sure you don't forget anything because it's a helluva walk back to the car, especially in the dark. It's got a restroom with old vault toilets and each camp spot has a fire ring, a table, and an old wood stove with a chimney. Interesting although we didn't use it as it looked like too much work, plus what are you gonna cook on it? Steak? Eggs? Chicken and shrimp fajitas? Hmm come to think of it, that doesn't sound so bad! Bring a water pump filter to drink. Lots of shade here with tall trees overhead nice n cool. River runs next to it and a few different trails intersect here taking you to different places, other campgrounds and even Mt. Wilson. I recommend at least a couple nights. I stayed here 3 days with my then girlfriend. Great spot!< /review>< pictures>

<Response>None</Response>< Review>
Simple, Affordable, and Convenient! You can't expect any more from a storage facility. From day one, I have not encountered any problems whatsoever. With a "simple to set-up" online access account, making payments is a breeze and I can even add authorized users or update my contact info since I was in the process of relocating. I did fall behind from my payments at one point and my lock was cut, but I can't blame them since I was a "no call, no show" for almost 2 months. It is company policy just like any other storage company would. I have been renting at this Public Storage for six months. I have an outside storage (outside the gated entrance) which I can conveniently access 24/7 and I have not had any problems (knock on wood) with loss, theft or damage to any of my belongings. It is located in an industrial part of Sun Valley and just blocks away from the local police department. As long as you don't mind the traffic and noise from the semi-trucks, you could be assured that your storage will be safe. Best of all, the property manager, Dayann, is doing an excellent job keeping this place safe, clean, and in order. My overall experience, I give this property 5-stars! I definitely would recommend this location to all.< /Review>
